NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

S. Subiramaniyam male child born to Srinivasan, (No. 00115/09 District Social Welfare Office, Kanyakumari)
Who is residing at No. 58, Kalingar Street, Thiyagi Kumaran Street, Coimbatore-641 001, was Physically examined on
4th May 1999 at Coimbatore Medical College Hospital, Coimbatore. Has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual
reassignment surgery by Dr. K. Mahadevan, Professor of STD Coimbatore Medical College Hospital, Coimbatore-641 018.
By this she may be treated as a female and shall hence forth be known as S. SUBIKSHA.
